msg:Let me first say the conclusion. For a hotel with obvious advantages and disadvantages, you need to make a plan in advance and think clearly about your needs so as not to affect your mood for travel.
The biggest feature of this hotel is that it is very close to tourist attractions (the hotel itself is a tourist attraction). It is not far from Liuxiang Bell Tower Street, which is convenient for eating, staying and playing. The night view of the hotel is nothing to say. It has the local tyrant style of Shanxi Jinshang Courtyard. It is no problem to upload 10 more photos. The hotel lobby is very grand and check-in is fast. Jinsheng Building is the main building of the hotel. There is a small door next to it that allows you to swipe the room card directly to Wenying Lake Park. Jinfulou is a restaurant, and the price is higher than outside.
As for the accommodation conditions, it can be said to be relatively old, the room is not big, the 20-square-meter room is a bit small, and the layout is also relatively old-fashioned. The porcelain basin in my room is still cracked. But the service is okay, and there is more water, which can be taken in the corridor. The breakfast is rich in variety, and Fenjiu is indeed provided, but the head needs to be ordered a la carte, the price is the same as outside.
In summary, this is an older hotel. The service has been tried, but due to the limitation of hardware facilities, it cannot be further improved. The interior needs major renovation. For travel, you need to prepare your psychological expectations in advance so as not to be too disappointed.

msg:It has a sense of history. Both Xu Zhimo and Premier Zhou Enlai have been there.

I waited for more than an hour to clean the room that day. No one informed me that I could check in. I had to ask myself. Fortunately, I could sit in the lobby tea bar for a while. I could rest without ordering anything. The service was very good. Later, I ordered tea and was given a cup of flower tea.

The room was close to the road when I entered it. Unfortunately, the municipal government was repairing the road, which was very noisy. I called the front desk to ask for a solution. A girl was sent to say that it could not be solved. Then, seeing my firm attitude, she said she would ask the supervisor. After waiting for a while, there was still no feedback. I could only call the front desk to confirm. The front desk told me that the municipal government could not interfere. Otherwise, I could move to a small standard room. In the end, I asked myself whether there was a room a little further away from the road. Only then did I say that I could go and see if it was vacant. However, the girl who came to handle it earlier told me that there was no room. This operation was also very confusing.
The hotel room was generally OK, but the drainage was too bad. When I took a shower, the water flowed all over the outside. The water in the sink could not go down, and flushing the toilet was even worse.
Fruits were delivered every day, and the breakfast was OK. It was rich for this price. The night view was super beautiful and very photogenic.
The restaurant of the hotel is a popular restaurant on the Internet. There is a queue every day. The waiter was very considerate to remind that there is a 15% service charge for delivery, but not for take-out. Later, we ordered donkey meat rolls and fried meat, which were both delicious.
Nearby is Taiyuan Station and May Day Square. The hotel room card can go to Chunyang Palace for free, which is also on the side, but we didn't go because of time. Bell Tower Street and Causeway Bay Plaza are also on the side, so it's nice to go shopping.
We encountered a wedding on the day of leaving the hotel. The gongs and drums were very ceremonial. The only thing was that many people living opposite us smoked in the corridor, and the smell of smoke was smoked as soon as the door opened.
Overall, it's good, but it would be better if we paid more attention to the details.

There are many windows in the room, and it is very troublesome to draw the curtains. It is recommended to replace them with electric curtains. Also, the window switch is really high. I can't reach it with my 170cm tall hand. The light in the room is very dark. Even if all the lights are turned on, it feels like my eyes are still open when looking at the mobile phone. Uncomfortable, this is where it falls short. In terms of room facilities, I was surprised that the disposable slippers were the same as those in Yingze Hotel and were charged for taking them away. However, I called Yingze Hotel and asked if they could take them away for free, but Shanxi Hotel I called and was told that there was only one kind of disposable slippers. I always felt that they were not disposable and would be recycled, disinfected, cleaned and reused, which was very uncomfortable. The bedding and sofa are very soft, which I like. Although there are many windows in the room, almost nothing can be seen outside the windows. Maybe because it is an ancient building, and it feels like it is surrounded by private houses.
